TI RADIATIVE BREAKING OF PECCEI-QUINN SYMMETRY AT THE INTERMEDIATE MASS
   SCALE
SO PHYSICS LETTERS B
LA English
DT Article
ID SOLAR-NEUTRINO PROBLEM; STRONG CP-PROBLEM; POSSIBLE EXPLANATION;
   PARTICLE PHYSICS; INVISIBLE AXION; OSCILLATIONS; SUPERSYMMETRY;
   CONSERVATION; COSMOLOGY; INFLATION
AB We construct a supersymmetric (SUSY) extension of an invisible axion model, in which the Peccei-Quinn symmetry is broken naturally at the intermediate mass scale 10(10)-10(12) GeV by radiative corrections from right-handed neutrino loops. The SUSY-invariant mass of doublet Higgs supermultiplets is forbidden by the Peccei-Quinn symmetry, whose breading, however, generates an invariant Higgs mass of the order of the Fermi scale. In this model the right-handed neutrinos acquire large Majorana masses which are in a favored range for the Mikheyev-Smimov-Wolfenstein solution to the solar neutrino problem.

TI PECCEI-QUINN SYMMETRY AND SUPPRESSION OF NUCLEON-DECAY RATES IN
   SUSY-GUTS
SO PHYSICS LETTERS B
LA English
DT Article
ID SUPERSYMMETRIC PARTICLES; UNIFIED THEORIES; Z0 DECAYS; SEARCH; LIMITS;
   MASSES; CONSERVATION; ELECTROWEAK; UNIFICATION; COLLISIONS
AB We construct a supersymmetric grand unified model with a Peccei-Quinn symmetry. The dimension-five operators for baryon-number violation are suppressed by the Peccei-Quinn symmetry. We show that the dimension-five operators can be made much below the upper bound from the present nucleon-decay experiments, keeping superparticles at less than or similar 1 TeV which may be necessity for the supersymmetry to be a solution to the mass hierarchy problem. However, the dimension-five operators cannot be arbitrarily small due to the requirement of the unification of gauge coupling constants.

TI PROBING THE GRAND-UNIFICATION-SCALE MASS-SPECTRUM THROUGH
   PRECISION-MEASUREMENTS ON THE WEAK-SCALE PARAMETERS
SO PHYSICAL REVIEW LETTERS
LA English
DT Article
ID NUCLEON-DECAY; SUPERSYMMETRIC GUTS; UNIFIED THEORIES; ELECTROWEAK;
   BREAKING; LIFETIME; MODELS; LIMITS; SU(5)
AB We study the renormalization-group evolution of gauge coupling constants including mass threshold effects of both light and heavy particles, in the minimal supersymmetric SU(5) grand unified model assuming supersymmetry breaking at less than or similar to 1 TeV. We show that a certain combination of superheavy masses M(V)2M(SIGMA) is tightly constrained, while the mass of the color-triplet Higgs boson, M(H), can vary from 2 x 10(13) to 2 x 10(17) GeV. With a relatively heavy color-triplet mass (M(H) is similar to 10(17) GeV), the present nucleon-decay experiments still allow superparticles below 1 TeV. The importance of a precise measurement on alpha-3 is stressed.

TI SOLUTIONS TO THE TAU-LIFETIME PROBLEM
SO PHYSICS LETTERS B
LA English
DT Article
ID PARTICLE
AB We explore the origin of the disparity between the experiment of the tau-leptonic decay lifetime and the value predicted from e-mu-tau-universality. We discuss that there are basically only three possibilities, including the new possibility that two SU (2)L triplet scalars interfere destructively with the W-exchange in the tau-decay.

TI NEUTRINO DARK MATTER WITH A GALACTIC-RANGE NEW FORCE
SO MODERN PHYSICS LETTERS A
LA English
DT Article
AB We propose a new force of the galactic range acting among massive neutrinos to weaken the phase space constraint for the neutrino dark halo. As a consequence we find that the neutrino with mass 10 eV becomes a candidate for the galaxy dark halo to explain the observed flat rotation curves. Cosmological consequence of the new force is briefly discussed. It is, furthermore, pointed out that the new force can be naturally incorporated into the see-saw model for the neutrino mass.

TI CAN THE STRONGLY INTERACTING DARK MATTER BE A HEATING SOURCE OF JUPITER
SO PROGRESS OF THEORETICAL PHYSICS
LA English
DT Article
ID PHASE-TRANSITION; GALAXY; MASS
AB We show that the strongly-interacting massive particle (SIMP) with mass of 3 x 10(6) - 10(7) GeV is astrophysically interesting as a dark matter candidate in the galactic halo.  The annihilation of SIMPs inside Jupiter naturally explains the intrinsic heat flux irrespective of details of the planetary models.  We discuss its effect in all Jovian planets as well as in the Sun and the Earth.  We also comment that such a SIMP is accommodated in a class of hadronic axion models.

TI VIABLE SU(5) GUT WITH LIGHT LEPTOQUARK BOSONS
SO MODERN PHYSICS LETTERS A
LA English
DT Article
AB It is shown that the standard SU(5) GUT survives all experimental constraints if one introduces a pair of leptoquark bosons at the Fermi scale approximately O(100) GeV.  This model predicts tau(p --> e+ pi(0)) = 7 x 10(29) -7 x 10(32) yr which is marginally allowed by the present proton decay experiments and lies in the range testable at the super-Kamiokande.

TI VANISHING SQUARK AND SLEPTON MASSES IN A CLASS OF SUPERGRAVITY MODELS
SO PHYSICAL REVIEW D
LA English
DT Article
ID BROKEN SUPERSYMMETRIC THEORIES; WEAK-SYMMETRY-BREAKING; NO-SCALE
   SUPERGRAVITY; YANG-MILLS THEORIES; NEUTRAL CURRENTS; STANDARD MODEL;
   GAUGE-THEORIES; Z0 DECAYS; ENERGY; GUTS
AB We study a class of supergravity models where an observable sector is separated from a hidden sector in the superspace density which defines the supergravity Lagrangian.  It is shown that soft supersymmetry-breaking mass terms for squarks and sleptons vanish at the tree level if the cosmological constant vanishes.  Since their masses are induced by radiative corrections mostly due to gauge interactions, the sfermions with the same gauge-quantum numbers are highly degenerate in mass, which is required for the suppression of the flavor-changing neutral currents.  By a numerical calculation, we find that the SU(2)L x U(1)Y gauge symmetry can be broken by quantum corrections for suitable values of the free parameters.  Some phenomenological features of this model are investigated.  In particular, this model predicts right-handed sleptons below 150 GeV.
RP INOUE, K (reprint author), TOHOKU UNIV,DEPT PHYS,SENDAI,MIYAGI 980,JAPAN.
RI Yanagida, Tsutomu/A-4394-2011

TI MASS DEGENERACY OF SQUARKS AND SLEPTONS IN SUPERGRAVITY

LA English

AB Mass degeneracy of squarks and sleptons is discussed in the framework of Einstein supergravity. TI SUB-PICONEWTON FORCE FLUCTUATIONS OF ACTOMYOSIN INVITRO
SO NATURE
LA English
DT Article
ID SINGLE KINESIN MOLECULES; ACTIN-FILAMENTS; MUSCLE-CONTRACTION; SLIDING
   FILAMENTS; MYOSIN; MOVEMENT; MECHANISM; MOTION; DIRECTION; VELOCITY
AB A new system has been developed for measuring the forces produced by a small number (< 5-150) of myosin molecules interacting with a single actin filament in vitro. The technique can resolve forces of less than a piconewton and has a time resolution in the submillisecond range. It can thus detect fluctuations of force caused by individual molecular interactions. From analysis of these force fluctuations, the coupling between the enzymatic ATPase activity of actomyosin and the resulting mechanical impulses can be elucidated.

TI RENORMALIZATION-GROUP ANALYSIS ON THE HIGGS MASS IN THE SOFTLY-BROKEN
   SUPERSYMMETRIC STANDARD MODEL
SO PHYSICS LETTERS B
LA English
DT Article
ID SYMMETRY-BREAKING; SUPERGRAVITY; ENERGY
AB We calculate a mass of the lightest Higgs boson in the minimal supersymmetric standard model by solving one-loop renormalization-group equations. In the range m(t) = 150-200 GeV and for a supersymmetry breaking scale m(SUSY) = 1-100 TeV the mass m(H0) varies from 70 GeV to 190 GeV. A possibility to probe the supersymmetry breaking scale is also discussed.

TI HEAVY AXION ON SARK BRIDGE BETWEEN HIGGS AND TECHNICOLOR MODELS
SO MODERN PHYSICS LETTERS A
LA English
DT Article
AB It is shown how imposition of Peccei-Quinn symmetry leads to a heavy axion and strong constraints in the sark model.  The axion and sark masses are derived.  Analysis of chiral symmetry breaking leads to mass formulae for pseudo-Goldstone bosons; the lightest is between 44 and 125 GeV.  A general picture which bridges between the sark model and a technicolor model, in terms of a new angle, is proposed.

TI PARTIALLY BROKEN SEESAW MECHANISM
SO PHYSICAL REVIEW LETTERS
LA English
DT Article
ID BETA-DECAY; HEAVY NEUTRINOS; 17-KEV NEUTRINO; SEARCH; S-35; SPECTRUM
AB In a class of models with global SU(n) family symmetry, the possibility naturally exists that n - 1 generations have light neutrinos and the remaining generation has a medium-heavy neutrino, of the order of the charged-lepton mass or the quark mass, as a consequence of an incomplete action of the seesaw mechanism.  We discuss as applications two possibilities:  (i) The heavy neutrino is identified with the neutral particle of mass 17 keV suggested by Simpson from beta-decay experiments, and (ii) there may exist a fourth generation and the associated neutrino has a heavy mass, probably of the order of a hundred GeV.

TI SIMPSONS HEAVY NEUTRINO AND THE MAJORANA NEUTRINO HYPOTHESIS
SO PROGRESS OF THEORETICAL PHYSICS
LA English
DT Article
ID BETA-DECAY; 17-KEV NEUTRINO; S-35; SPECTRUM; SEARCH; EMISSION; LIMITS;
   WIDTH; MASS; Z0
AB If the neutral particle with a mass of 17keV found by Simpson is identified with one of the neutrinos of the Majorana type, strong constraints are derived on the neutrino mass matrix from existing experiments on neutrinoless double beta decays and neutrino oscillations.  In particular we found that m-nu-mu congruent-to (180-250) keV with sin2(2)-THETA-nu(e)-nu-mu congruent-to 0.002-0.003.  The presence of the second-generation right-handed neutrino is also predicted at around the mass of M approximately 50 GeV with the aid of the seesaw mechanism.
